        </summary>

        <ul class="dropdown-menu dropdown-menu-sw" style="width: 175px">

        <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-quick-reference" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#quick-reference"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Quick reference</h1>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Def</th>
<th>Desc</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>IP Address</td>
<td><ul dir="auto"><li>Internet Protocol Address</li> <li>Unique point-of-attachment on Internet (like GPS), but <strong>no Geographical order</strong></li></ul></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="#dns">DNS server</a></td>
<td><ul dir="auto"><li>Domain Name System/Service/Servers</li><li>Obtain IP address from hostname - computer know multiple </li></ul></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Default Gateway</td>
<td>Where to send pkg</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="#dhcp">DHCP</a></td>
<td>Dynamic Host Configuration Protocol</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Host</td>
<td><ul dir="auto"><li>computers and applications that communicate over the internet</li><li>considered on the edge of the network</li></ul></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Routers</td>
<td><ul dir="auto"><li>carrying communication btw host</li><li>core of the internet</li></ul></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="#socket">Socket</a></td>
<td><code>IP addr + port</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="#connection">Connection</a></td>
<td>Uniquely identified by a pair of sockets</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="#port-number">Port number</a></td>
<td>65535 ports</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="#protocol-stack-tcpip">Protocol Stack</a></td>
<td>a group of softwares where each has its own role</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="#tcp">TCP</a></td>
<td>Transmission Control Protocol</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="#udp">UDP</a></td>
<td>User Datagram Protocol</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>FQDN</td>
<td>Fully Qualified Domain Name</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>frame</td>
<td>L2 unit of exchange</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Network Interface</td>
<td>The point of interconnection between a computer and a private or public network</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-introduction" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#introduction"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Introduction</h1>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-how-to-connect" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-to-connect"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>How to connect</h2>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Query DNS server for IP Address</li>
<li>See if local (on same wifi,...) by <a href="#longest-prefix-matching">looking at the first 64 bits of the IP address</a> (should be identical)</li>
<li>Initiate connection via <code>Default Gateway</code></li>
</ol>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-dhcp" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dhcp"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>DHCP</h2>
<p dir="auto"><em>To obtain Configuration Params</em></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>DHCP: <code>broadcast</code> to everyone on the same network (<code>DHCP discover message</code>) for help</li>
<li>DHCP server provides <code>DHCP offer</code>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>IP address</li>
<li>Gateway</li>
<li>DNS servers</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><em>(If client accept)</em> DHCP request</li>
<li>DHCP acknowledgement
<ul dir="auto">
<li>IP address, gateway, DNS servers</li>
<li>Timeout (must contact DHCP to renew)</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">Network contains:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Application usings the network</li>
<li>Routers, Switches, Hubs</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-basic-concepts" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#basic-concepts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Basic concepts:</h1>
<p dir="auto">Networking: 2 different buffered layer activities</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Network programming: Writing applications that are connecting other applications, are communicating as part of how they accomplish their objectives, and are exposed and visible to the user
<ul dir="auto">
<li>eg: webclient that connects to and comminucates with a server</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Network formation: Making sure that the internet can carry these connection</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-unicast--multicast--anycast" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#unicast--multicast--anycast"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Unicast / Multicast / Anycast</h2>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-unicast" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#unicast"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><a href="#unicast">Unicast</a>:</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>exactly 1 sender, exactly 1 recipient (send and receive a response from a specific webserver)</li>
<li>Universally supported (any computers can use)</li>
<li>Sender and recipient uniquely identified (IP is part of this)</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-multicast" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#multicast"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Multicast:</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>1 sender, a set of recipient (DHCP)</li>
<li>Generally supported natively only on local area network
<ul dir="auto">
<li>To avoid spamming</li>
<li>Managing is very hard</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Will not be forwarded outside the LAN by ADSL or fiber module or routers, but circulate freely inside the LAN</li>
<li>Sender uniquely identified, recipients NAMED but UNKNOWN (with an identifier on address)</li>
<li>eg: Chromecast, Multicast Adr Range (IPv4: 224.0.0.0 - 239.255.255.255, IPv6: ffoo::/8)</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-anycast" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#anycast"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Anycast:</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>1 sender wishes to send a msg to one amongst the set of recipients who share the same identifiers (<code>IP Address</code>)</li>
<li>Really just Unicast</li>
<li>Have an <code>IP addr</code> for <code>src</code> and <code>dst</code></li>
<li>Internet core will route a pkg from <code>src</code> to the nearest <code>host</code> with the <code>dst IP addr</code></li>
<li>Typically used scarely for routing</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>IF WANTS TO CONNECT TO A SET OF HOST OVER THE INTERNET, USE MANY UNICAST CONNECTIONS</strong></p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-unicast-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#unicast-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Unicast</h1>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-identifier" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#identifier"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Identifier:</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Machine + Process: <code>IPaddr:port</code> -&gt; <a href="#socket"><code>Socket</code></a></li>
<li>For TCP and UDP,</li>
<li>Process identified by port</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-socket" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#socket"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Socket:</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>IPaddr:port</code></li>
<li>Endpoint for communication</li>
<li>Uniquely identifies a process in the Internet</li>
<li>Described as tuple: <code>(IPaddr, port)</code></li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-connection" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#connection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Connection:</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Uniquely identified by a pair of sockets</li>
<li>For a given transport protocol: <code>(IPaddr1, port1, IPadrr2, port2)</code></li>
<li>Completely: <code>({TCP | UDP}, IPaddr1, port1, IPaddr2, port2)</code> across the Internet
-&gt; Identify to which connection any pkg belongs</li>
<li>Possible to have 2 clients <code>(IPaddr1, port1) and (IPaddr2, port2)</code> connects to the same host (IPadrr3, port3)</li>
<li>? Can 2 connections with same IP and port but with different protocol? -&gt; NO for TCP but YES for UDP!</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-port-number" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#port-number"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Port number:</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Have semantics agreed upon by IANA (80: http,..., 15345: xPilot)</li>
<li>Default port 80</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-connection-phases" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#connection-phases"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Connection phases:</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Set up connection
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Server listens on a port (<code>passive open</code>) - Accept incoming conn. reqs</li>
<li>Client connects to server (initiate) (<code>active open</code>) -&gt; <code>Client != Server</code> at who takes initiative - Generate conn req</li>
<li>Handshake - Negotiate conn. params</li>
</ol>
</li>
<li>Transit data back-and-forth: read from socket, write to socket</li>
<li>Either can tear down the connection</li>
</ol>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-protocol-stack-tcpip" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#protocol-stack-tcpip"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Protocol Stack (TCP/IP):</h1>
<p dir="auto"><em>A group of softwares where each has its own role</em></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>(Data)Link layer (2)</strong>: <em>"Get data across a <code>link (1 hop)</code>     "</em>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>functions that allows communicate through a single link directly to another computer or router</li>
<li><em>Who knows</em>: try to make transmission but with no guarantee that will succeed (eg. may not be connected)</li>
<li><strong>HEADER &amp; FOOTER:</strong> <code>Ethertype (L2 header element)</code> - IPv4, IPv6,...
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Contains FOOTER to signal ends of transfer, and checksum</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>eg: Ethernet, Wifi, Token Ring, ATM, Avian carrier</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>(Inter)Network(ing) Layer (3)</strong>: <em>"get data across a <code>multi-hop</code> network"</em>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>for a pkg, which interface should I send the pkg so that it gets close to the dest</li>
<li>Computer doesn't have a choice (must send through wifi)</li>
<li>But ADSL or fiber module does (typically has ethernet interfaces and WAN ports (connects to the internet)), so has to decide whether to send over the Ethernet or WAN port)</li>
<li><em>Best Effort service</em>: tries to find an interface to forward the pkg, but it may not know which and drop the pkg, or send to Layer 2, which fails</li>
<li><strong>HEADER:</strong> <code>Protocol number (IPv4/IPv6 header element)</code></li>
<li>eg: IP</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Transport layer (4)</strong>: <em>"Ensuring End-to-End Properties"</em>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Protocols such as TCP, UDP</li>
<li>Each protocol provides a <em>well-defined</em> transport service to other layers
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Transport layer is in charge of how incoming pkg are delivered to the receiving application</li>
<li>May has well-defined transport semantic (1 2 3 or 3 2 1 or FIFO)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>HEADER:</strong> Port number (TCP, UDP header element)</li>
<li><strong>! RAW IP protocol ignores layer 4</strong></li>
<li>The checksum is for End-to-End integrity opposed to data-link checksum is for link integrity.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Application Data (7)</strong>: <em>"Application specific exchanges"</em></li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/nhat-vo/CSE207/blob/main/final/img/osi-model-7-layers.svg"><img src="/nhat-vo/CSE207/raw/main/final/img/osi-model-7-layers.svg" alt="protocol stack" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-type-of-protocol" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#type-of-protocol"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Type of protocol</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Datalink layer: Ethertype
<ul dir="auto">
<li>wifi</li>
<li>Ethernet</li>
<li>Token Ring</li>
<li>ATM</li>
<li>Avian Carrier</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Network layer: Protocol number
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ICMP=1</li>
<li>TCP=6</li>
<li>UDP=17</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Port number:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>IMAP=143</li>
<li>HTTP=80</li>
<li>SMTP=25</li>
<li>IRC</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-tcp" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tcp"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>TCP</h1>
<p dir="auto"><em>Transport layer protocol</em></p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-semantics" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#semantics"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Semantics:</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Provide applications with end-to-end transport semantics:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Present data to receiving application <em>AS THEY WERE SENT</em></li>
<li>Preserve ordering, ensure reliability &amp; integrity (with restransmission/reordering)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Assumptions:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>Best Effort</em> from Network layer (reordering, loss, garbling possible)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><em>Connection oriented</em>: must negotiate conn params before any data can flow
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Buffers and timeout for retransmission</li>
<li>Sequence numbers (how to enumerate the data)</li>
<li>Checksum (integrity)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Not Multicast-capable</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-process" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#process"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Process:</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Server <code>bind</code> (associate a socket with an addr) and <code>listen</code> (prepare the socket for incoming conn) to a port, <code>accepting</code> (when conn finally arrives) incoming conn reqs</li>
<li>Clients connects to server</li>
<li>Handshake</li>
</ol>
<details><summary><h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-code" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#code"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Code</h3></summary>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// COMMON
// create socket
// socket(&lt;addr family&gt;,&lt;protocol type&gt;,&lt;protocol variation&gt;)
int mysocket = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_STREAM, 0);


// SERVER-SIDE
// associate socket with addr &amp; port
bind(mysocket, (struct sockaddr*)&amp;serv, sizeof(struct sockaddr));

// listen for incoming connections
// listen(&lt;socket&gt;, &lt;length of queue&gt;)
listen(mysocket, 2);

// accept connection
int consocket = accept(mysocket, (struct sockaddr*)&amp;dest, &amp;socksize);


// CLIENT-SIDE
// connect to a host
connect(mysocket, (struct sockaddr*) dst, sizeof(sockaddr_in));


// COMMON
// transfer data...
send(mysocket, msg, strlen(msg), 0);

// close connection
close(socket);

/**
struct sockaddr {
		portnumber,
		IP addr of machine
}
**/"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> COMMON</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> create socket</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> socket(&lt;addr family&gt;,&lt;protocol type&gt;,&lt;protocol variation&gt;)</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> mysocket = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_STREAM, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);


<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> SERVER-SIDE</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> associate socket with addr &amp; port</span>
<span class="pl-en">bind</span>(mysocket, (<span class="pl-k">struct</span> sockaddr*)&amp;serv, sizeof(<span class="pl-k">struct</span> sockaddr));

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> listen for incoming connections</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> listen(&lt;socket&gt;, &lt;length of queue&gt;)</span>
<span class="pl-en">listen</span>(mysocket, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> accept connection</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> consocket = accept(mysocket, (<span class="pl-k">struct</span> sockaddr*)&amp;dest, &amp;socksize);


<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> CLIENT-SIDE</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> connect to a host</span>
<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(mysocket, (<span class="pl-k">struct</span> sockaddr*) dst, sizeof(sockaddr_in));


<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> COMMON</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> transfer data...</span>
<span class="pl-en">send</span>(mysocket, msg, strlen(msg), 0);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> close connection</span>
<span class="pl-en">close</span>(socket);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span>*</span>
<span class="pl-c">struct sockaddr {</span>
<span class="pl-c">		portnumber,</span>
<span class="pl-c">		IP addr of machine</span>
<span class="pl-c">}</span>
<span class="pl-c">*<span class="pl-c">*/</span></span></pre></div>
</details>
<details><summary>Note</summary>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>accept</code> is blocking, but <code>mysocket</code> could be made to non-blocking</li>
<li><code>bind</code> can be made to listen to all ports on the machine</li>
<li><code>socket</code> can use other addr family than IP</li>
</ul>
</details>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-diagram" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#diagram"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Diagram</h3>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1fcb576b698b9c0dba8204c70c5af6674a9e4cf25147c8851bb5a59e100223a4/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6765656b73666f726765656b732e6f72672f77702d636f6e74656e742f75706c6f6164732f536f636b65745f7365727665722d312e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1fcb576b698b9c0dba8204c70c5af6674a9e4cf25147c8851bb5a59e100223a4/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6765656b73666f726765656b732e6f72672f77702d636f6e74656e742f75706c6f6164732f536f636b65745f7365727665722d312e706e67" alt="TCP process diagram. Note we can add close on both sides on the bottom" data-canonical-src="https://media.geeksforgeeks.org/wp-content/uploads/Socket_server-1.png" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-udp" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#udp"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>UDP</h1>
<p dir="auto"><em>Transport layer protocol</em></p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-semantics-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#semantics-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Semantics</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>Minimum Service</em> - guarantee only integrity (<code>checksum</code>) -&gt; <strong>unreliable</strong></li>
<li>Multicast-capable, local set-up only, multi-client/connection-less</li>
<li>Assumptions:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>Best effort</em>: reordering, loss, garbling possible</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>No difference between client/server</li>
<li><strong>Connection-less</strong> - no handshake/setup</li>
<li>Presents packets as they arrive, no ordering guarantee</li>
</ul>
<details><summary><h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-code-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#code-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Code</h3></summary>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// create socket
// socket(&lt;addr family&gt;,&lt;protocol type&gt;,&lt;protocol variation&gt;)
int mysocket = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_DGRAM, 0);

// send to dst - no connection required
sendto(mysocket, const void *msg, int len, unsigned int flags, const struct sockaddr *dst, socklen_t dstsize);"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> create socket</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> socket(&lt;addr family&gt;,&lt;protocol type&gt;,&lt;protocol variation&gt;)</span>
<span class="pl-k">int</span> mysocket = socket(AF_INET, SOCK_DGRAM, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>);

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> send to dst - no connection required</span>
<span class="pl-en">sendto</span>(mysocket, <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> *msg, <span class="pl-k">int</span> len, <span class="pl-k">unsigned</span> <span class="pl-k">int</span> flags, <span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-k">struct</span> sockaddr *dst, <span class="pl-c1">socklen_t</span> dstsize);</pre></div>
</details>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-diagram-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#diagram-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Diagram</h3>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/15a69088bd1429479f30627bf893a53e2f7578b128a36ad44e82626a54daac79/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6765656b73666f726765656b732e6f72672f77702d636f6e74656e742f63646e2d75706c6f6164732f32303232303530343137303730372f7365727665722d616e642d636c69656e742e6a7067"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/15a69088bd1429479f30627bf893a53e2f7578b128a36ad44e82626a54daac79/68747470733a2f2f6d656469612e6765656b73666f726765656b732e6f72672f77702d636f6e74656e742f63646e2d75706c6f6164732f32303232303530343137303730372f7365727665722d616e642d636c69656e742e6a7067" alt="UDP diagram" data-canonical-src="https://media.geeksforgeeks.org/wp-content/cdn-uploads/20220504170707/server-and-client.jpg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-indentifiers" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#indentifiers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Indentifiers</h1>
<p dir="auto"><em>To identify, unambiguously, 1 single resource on the Internet</em></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>http://www.example.com:80/filename.html</code></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>FQDN: <code>www.example.com</code></li>
<li>DNS Lookup to find IP addr</li>
<li>Find a path to the router of destination</li>
<li>Lookup L2 addr of destination (in ARP(IPv4)/Neighbor(IPv6) Table - match IP addr - L2 addr)</li>
<li>(if no entry) <em>broadcast</em> <code>Neighbor Solicitation (IPv6)</code> or <code>ARP who-has (IPv4)</code>-&gt; Device <em>unicast</em> its L2 with <code>Neighbor Advertisement</code> or <code>ARP is-at</code> -&gt; router updates <em>ARP/Neighbor table</em> and switch update <em>switching</em> and</li>
<li>Generate frame with L2 (not IP) addr and send to switch -&gt; switch send to computer</li>
<li>Use <code>Ethertype</code> (from L2), <code>Protocol Number</code> (from L3), and <code>Port Number</code> (from L4) to send to application</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>L2 addr (MAC addr, Hardware addr): match IP addr to L2 addr</li>
<li>Identify one single resource on the Internet.</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-dns" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>DNS</h1>
<p dir="auto"><a href="#how-to-connect"><em>How to get the IP addr of <code>facebook.com</code>?</em></a></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Query <strong>DNS server</strong> -&gt; IP addr</li>
<li>Whether destination is local -&gt; whether 2 IP addr are similar (first 64 bits)</li>
<li>Initiate connection via default gateway (sending the pkg)</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-history" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#history"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>History</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ARPANET - few hosts connected, IPv4 addr are hard to remember</li>
<li>Solution: HOSTS.TXT (win) - /etc/hosts (Linux)
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>&lt;name&gt;:&lt;IPaddr&gt;</code></li>
<li>Manually maintained by SRI-NIC</li>
<li>Manually copied to all hosts on ARPANET</li>
<li>On a "good faith" principle - assume that updates are correct</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Problem:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Didn't scale</li>
<li>Out-of-date info</li>
<li>Anyone could <em>break</em> by rogue updates</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-purposes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#purposes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Purposes</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Mapping btw hostnames and IP addresses
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Name:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>hierarchically structured namespace</li>
<li>single-source for autoritative corresponding</li>
<li>de-centralised management</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>IP Address (actually record): include (type, value, lifetime)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Handling transitions btw IPv4 and IPv6</li>
<li>Resource-sharing</li>
<li>Load-sharing/balancing</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-summary" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#summary"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Summary</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>A distributed databased</li>
<li>Hierarchically structured name-space
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Single-source for authoritative corresponding <code>&lt;record&gt;</code></li>
<li>decentralized management</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>&lt;record&gt;</code>: <code>(type, value, lifetime)</code></li>
<li>Note: name -&gt; (type, value, lifetime) just for explanation, for more detail look at <a href="#dns-resource-records">DNS Resource Records</a></li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-dns-name-space" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dns-name-space"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>DNS Name Space:</h1>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>FQDN (Fully Qualified Domain Name):
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Unique location in DNS tree</li>
<li>edge == . (! must have trailing dot)</li>
<li>written right to left</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Authorative Zone:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Only update a local table</li>
<li>Points to next node</li>
<li>Table of name and record is called <code>Zone file</code>
<em>It's really just a tree</em></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-fqdn" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#fqdn"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>FQDN:</h3>
<p dir="auto"><code>www.polytechnique.edu.</code></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Unique location in the DNS tree</li>
<li><code>.</code> corresponds to an edge</li>
<li>Written right to left</li>
<li>! must have a trailing dot</li>
<li>permits identifying unique location for <code>&lt;record&gt;</code></li>
<li>delegates responsibility for management of part of (a sub-tree of) the NS</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-organization" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#organization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Organization:</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><em>The root</em> - at the top - knows who to query for each name</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Each server maintains who is in charge of the record: <em>"is delegated to"</em> vs <em>"is authoritative for"</em></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Authorative Zone:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Only requires update a local table</li>
<li>Points to next node</li>
<li>The table of name and record is called <code>zone file</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-zone-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#zone-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Zone file:</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>name</th>
<th>record / redirect</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>net</td>
<td>NS:FQDN</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>edu</td>
<td>NS:FQDN</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>org</td>
<td>NS:FQDN</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-dns---name-resolution" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dns---name-resolution"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>DNS - Name resolution</h1>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-terminology" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#terminology"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Terminology</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Root DNS: Knows who is maintaining records for all given domains</li>
<li>Authoritative Server: Authoritative for a given domain (NS) - either response with the requested DNS resource record, or return an NS record to redirect to another server</li>
<li>Local DNS: query Root-DNS server and other DNS server on your behalf, typically is not authoritative for any name; may cache (&lt;= lifetime of record) (AKA: recursive resolver, local resolver, caching resolver)</li>
<li>Stub resolver: software on computer that interacts with local DNS server</li>
<li>Record: <code>(name, type, record, lifetime)</code></li>
<li>Recursive (local DNS) (<code>RA == 1</code>): automatically queries and redirects and return only the requested record</li>
<li>Non-recursive (all the others) (<code>RA == 0</code>): returns the authoritative servers if not authoritative for the record</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-querying-dns" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#querying-dns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Querying DNS</h3>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Computer queries Local DNS</li>
<li>Local DNS queries Root DNS -&gt; replies the authoritative server</li>
<li>Local DNS queries -&gt; authoritative server -&gt; ... -&gt; requested record</li>
<li>Local DNS caches all the authoritative server</li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-dig" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dig"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>dig</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>rd == 1</code>: recursion desired</li>
<li><code>ra == 1</code>: recursion available</li>
<li><code>AUTHORITY SECTION</code>: the servers authoritative for the name space</li>
<li><code>ADDITIONAL SECTION</code>: IP addr of the authoritative servers</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-dns-resource-records" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dns-resource-records"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>DNS Resource Records</h1>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Encoded in 2B ($2^{16}$ in total)</li>
<li><code>(NAME, TYPE) -&gt; (RECORD, LIFETIME)</code> (can be multiple)</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-dns-record-types" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dns-record-types"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>DNS Record types</h3>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Record Type</th>
<th>Name</th>
<th>Value</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A</td>
<td>FQDN</td>
<td>IPv4 addr</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>AAAA</td>
<td>FQDN</td>
<td>IPv6 addr</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CNAME</td>
<td>FQDN</td>
<td>Canonical name (alias) - FQDN</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MX (Mail exchange)</td>
<td>FQDN</td>
<td>Mailserver - (FQDN, priority)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TXT</td>
<td>FQDN</td>
<td>Random text</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>NS</td>
<td>FQDN</td>
<td>Authoritative Name server - (FQDN)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-mx-records" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#mx-records"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>MX Records</h3>
<p dir="auto"><code>user@sales.example.com</code></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Look at part behind <code>@</code></li>
<li>More than 1 MX record for the same name -&gt; try the ones with lowest priority number</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-dns---root-server" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dns---root-server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>DNS - Root server</h1>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>13 root server operators (identical) -&gt; numerous root server</li>
<li>Highly-available</li>
<li>Replicated</li>
<li><code>{a-m}.root-servers.net</code>.</li>
<li>"Bare" DNS server needs to know one (root, other) -&gt; can query other servers</li>
<li>Typically install list of all roots</li>
<li>Not just Root servers are replicated</li>
<li>Registration of FQDN requires guarantee that at least 2 name servers avilable to be authoritative - must be synchronized</li>
<li>Controlled by ICANN</li>
<li>alternative named.root exists (OpenNIC, ...), occasional conflicts and not all Internet users can access these domains</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-dns-and-the-protocol-stack" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dns-and-the-protocol-stack"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>DNS and the Protocol Stack</h1>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Application Layer Protocol (layer 7)</li>
<li>Usually uses UDP (can use TCP) - for speed
<ul dir="auto">
<li>No connection setup</li>
<li>No per-query-state</li>
<li>No per-client-state</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Format:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Pair request &amp; responses (identification)</li>
<li>Self-contained msg</li>
<li>Each msg can contain requests, records, or both</li>
<li>Interesting attack vectors</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-longest-prefix-matching" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#longest-prefix-matching"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Longest prefix matching</h1>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-terminology-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#terminology-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Terminology</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Prefix length</li>
<li>Prefix</li>
<li>Subnet</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-router" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#router"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Router:</h3>
<p dir="auto"><em>send through which interface to get closest to dst?</em></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>receive pkgs to network layer</li>
<li>consult routing table</li>
<li>send to interface with Longest Prefix Matching</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-routing-table" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#routing-table"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Routing table</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Dest - Next - Cost</li>
</ul>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-destination" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#destination"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Destination</h4>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Is a <a href="#subnet">subnet</a> or an IP Address</li>
</ul>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-next" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#next"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Next</h4>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Identified next router: Not the destination, but someone closer to the destination than I. eg: 129.104.11.1</li>
<li>Transmit over an interface: If the dest/next-hop exists, it's attached to the same link as this interface. eg: eth0, eth1</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-subnet" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#subnet"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Subnet</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>192.168.1.2/24: The 24 shows how many bits we care about the IP Address before</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-assumption" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#assumption"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Assumption:</h3>
<p dir="auto">Interfaces with IP addrs from within the same subnet prefix are on the same IP link (reachable in 1 IP hop, no router forward)</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-rules" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#rules"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Rules</h2>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Longest</li>
<li>Lowest cost</li>
</ol>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-local-link" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#local-link"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Local Link</h1>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-network-segment" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#network-segment"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Network Segment:</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Physical Entity</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Commonly assumed, a cable</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Constrained by physics</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Signal attenuation -&gt; Restrict length of segment</li>
<li><strong>Propagation delay</strong> -&gt; (Ideally) 1 transmitter at a time</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Station / Interface: Physical network interfaces on a cable</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Communication medium -&gt; signal may interfere</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Collision Domain</strong>: set of stations that may interfere</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Solution:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>MAC protocol</li>
<li>MUTEX - with no "hardware support"</li>
<li>More station, more contention, less throughput, longer delays</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-repeater" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#repeater"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Repeater</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Connect 2 cables</li>
<li>Each up-to max length</li>
<li>Regenerate &amp; amplify physical signal
-&gt; <strong>Allow segment to grow, unaffected by attenuation</strong></li>
<li>Extend collision domain</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-medium-access-control" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#medium-access-control"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Medium Access Control</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Exclusive access: only 1 station is transmitting at any point of time</li>
<li>Only have the shared communication medium available for collision detection</li>
</ul>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-rules-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#rules-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Rules:</h3>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><em>Listen before you transmit</em>: If a channel is busy, back-off</li>
<li><em>Listen while you transmit</em>:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>If transmission, other than own, received -&gt; COLLISON -&gt; back off, retry later</li>
<li>Otherwise, transmission succeeded</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Min transmission duration (min frame size) &gt; 2 * max propagation delay</li>
<li>Max network segment length -&gt; max # of repeaters:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>4 repeaters, 5 "cables"</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-bridge" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#bridge"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Bridge</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Connect 2 network segments
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Create disjoint collision domains</li>
<li>Participate on MAC protocol on each interface</li>
<li>Decodes receive signals into symbols (frames)</li>
<li>Keeps them in <strong>queues</strong></li>
<li>Attempt to send them with <em>Listen before/while you transmit</em>, retransmit if collision</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Listen to all received frames, record <code>&lt;addr, port&gt;</code> in <em>bridging table</em> (<em>port</em> here is not <em>port</em>)
<ul dir="auto">
<li>-&gt; learn which addr is reachable each port</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>When frame received over port <code>p_in</code> for addr <code>a</code>:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>if <code>&lt;a, p_out&gt;</code> does not exist in bridging table -&gt; forward over all ports except <code>p_in</code></li>
<li>if <code>&lt;a, p_out&gt;</code> exists:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>if <code>p_in == p_out</code> -&gt; do not forward</li>
<li>if <code>p_in != p_out</code> -&gt; forward to <code>p_out</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-in-real-world" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#in-real-world"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>In real world</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Switch == Bridge with multiple ports</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Each <code>port</code> is a separate collision domain</li>
<li>If single station/port -&gt; no collisions
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/nhat-vo/CSE207/blob/main/final/img/bridge.png"><img src="/nhat-vo/CSE207/raw/main/final/img/bridge.png" alt="repeater image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Hub == Repeater with multiple ports</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Regenerate signal but doesn't participate in the MAC protocol</li>
<li>Little used today
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/nhat-vo/CSE207/blob/main/final/img/repeater.png"><img src="/nhat-vo/CSE207/raw/main/final/img/repeater.png" alt="bridge image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-local-link-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#local-link-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Local Link</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Used to called network</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Link</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>set of interfaces which can communicate at L2 (not forwarded by a router)</li>
<li><strong>Broadcast capable</strong>: possible to make a transmission that will be received by all other computers on the same link (e.g DHCP discover)</li>
<li><strong>Explicit connectivity signals</strong>: I have (dis)connected from the server</li>
<li><strong>Full-broadcast, transitive, reflexive</strong></li>
<li>Unique identification of each station on a link - L2 addresses</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Separated by router (NOT switches or hubs)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Network</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Interfaces on 2 different networks (links) do not have full-broadcast, transitive, reflexive, connectivity</li>
<li>Unique identification of on which network (link) an interface is locate - IP addr</li>
<li>IP addr on the same link looks a like - share network prefix</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</article>
  </div>

    </div>

  </readme-toc>

</div>

  </div>


  </div>

  </turbo-frame>


    </main>
  </div>
